2024-10-30 09:02:54====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'e06d357e-e170-4233-8772-7c0661e80b93'
                            And a.事件id = '2EE96CD2-B23A-43E2-8F60-B9424143DF90'
                            And a.组序号 in (49)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-30 09:03:08====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'e06d357e-e170-4233-8772-7c0661e80b93'
                            And a.事件id = '2EE96CD2-B23A-43E2-8F60-B9424143DF90'
                            And a.组序号 in (51)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-30 09:13:50====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '45f351b8-8a69-4b38-90df-e911a45aae89'
                            And a.事件id = '7F640491-DA4F-4666-B6E6-018981742984'
                            And a.组序号 in (11)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-30 09:15:07====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '45f351b8-8a69-4b38-90df-e911a45aae89'
                            And a.事件id = '7F640491-DA4F-4666-B6E6-018981742984'
                            And a.组序号 in (16)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-30 09:18:25====>获取就诊信息:Select Decode(B.急诊,1,'2','1') As visitTypeCode,A.ID As visitNo,to_char(A.开始时间,'yyyymmdd') As visitDate,
                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,'' As wardCode,'' As wardName,'' As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人挂号记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D
                             Where A.Id=B.记录id And A.科室id=C.资源id And A.服务人id=D.资源id
                               And A.id='0D18625C-95C3-4F8D-9D71-F86B380E7C55'
                            Union All
                            Select '3' As visitTypeCode,A.ID As visitNo,to_char(A.开始时间,'yyyymmdd') As visitDate,
                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,E.编码 As wardCode,E.简称 As wardName,B.床号 As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人入院记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D,部门 E
                             Where A.Id=B.事件id And A.科室id=C.资源id And A.服务人id=D.资源id And B.病房id=E.资源id(+)
                               And A.id='0D18625C-95C3-4F8D-9D71-F86B380E7C55'
2024-10-30 09:18:25====>获取诊断信息:Select B.主诉 As chiefCompliant,C.问题名称 As diagName,C.问题编码 As diagCode
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人挂号记录 B,个人问题列表 C
                             Where A.Id=B.记录id And A.Id=C.服务记录id(+)
                               And A.id='0D18625C-95C3-4F8D-9D71-F86B380E7C55'
                               And Rownum<2
                            Union All
                            Select Distinct '' As chiefCompliant,C.问题名称 As diagName,C.问题编码 As diagCode
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人入院记录 B,个人问题列表 C
                             Where A.Id=B.事件id  And A.Id=C.服务记录id(+) And C.记录性质=2 
                               And A.id='0D18625C-95C3-4F8D-9D71-F86B380E7C55'
                               And Rownum<2

2024-10-30 09:18:27====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'ab1ed5c7-43a2-4ff2-bde4-13cee3420213'
                            And a.事件id = '0D18625C-95C3-4F8D-9D71-F86B380E7C55'
                            And a.组序号 in (11)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id

                        Order By sno

2024-10-30 09:30:36====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '45f351b8-8a69-4b38-90df-e911a45aae89'
                            And a.事件id = '7F640491-DA4F-4666-B6E6-018981742984'
                            And a.组序号 in (19)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))

2024-10-30 09:30:36====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '45f351b8-8a69-4b38-90df-e911a45aae89'
                            And a.事件id = '7F640491-DA4F-4666-B6E6-018981742984'
                            And a.组序号 in (21)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-30 11:05:27====>获取就诊信息:Select B.编码 As visit_departments,B.简称 As visit_departments_name,'1' As visit_type,A.Id As visit_no,'' As ward_code,'' As ward_name,'' As bed_no,nvl(D.保险号,'-') As medical_insurance_number
                          From 服务活动记录 A,部门 B,保险个人档案 D
                         Where A.Id='1FCC3AEE-131C-4988-BFC0-FD5766D4A82A'
                           And A.科室id=B.资源id And A.个人id=D.个人id(+)
                           And A.项目id='F4DA8ED2-5033-47EB-A08F-E442A5E65DAB'
                        Union All
                        Select B.编码 As visit_departments,B.简称 As visit_departments_name,'3' As visit_type,A.Id As visit_no,E.编码 As ward_code,E.简称 As ward_name,C.床号 As bed_no,nvl(D.保险号,'-') As medical_insurance_number
                          From 服务活动记录 A,部门 B,保险个人档案 D,个人当前状态 C,部门 E
                         Where A.Id='1FCC3AEE-131C-4988-BFC0-FD5766D4A82A'
                           And A.科室id=B.资源id And A.个人id=D.个人id(+) And A.Id=C.就诊id And C.病房id=E.资源id
                           And A.项目id='EC3E41BF-BACD-46BA-9D3C-E2493D73C1DF'
2024-10-30 11:05:27====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '0B386B57-CAC5-4768-B6ED-7D3BBB7A57DE'
                            And a.事件id = '1FCC3AEE-131C-4988-BFC0-FD5766D4A82A'
                            And a.组序号 in (14)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-30 11:05:28====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = '0B386B57-CAC5-4768-B6ED-7D3BBB7A57DE'
                            And a.事件id = '1FCC3AEE-131C-4988-BFC0-FD5766D4A82A'
                            And a.组序号 in (17)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-30 11:21:05====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242D3-BD7E-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = '74A7A4B9-932F-4C5B-9FE6-F46C76F5E9E1'
                            And a.组序号 in (12)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-30 11:21:05====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242D3-BD7E-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = '74A7A4B9-932F-4C5B-9FE6-F46C76F5E9E1'
                            And a.组序号 in (14)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242D3-BD7E-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = '74A7A4B9-932F-4C5B-9FE6-F46C76F5E9E1'
                            And a.组序号 in (16)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-10-30 12:14:30====>获取病人信息:Select A.Id As patientId,'01' As identityTypeCode,nvl(A.身份证号,'-') As identityNo,A.姓名 As personalName,A.性别 As sexCode,to_char(A.出生日期,'yyyymmdd') As birthDate,nvl(B.保险号,A.身份证号) As medicalCardNumber
                              From 个人信息 A,保险个人档案 B
                             Where A.Id=B.个人id(+) And B.系统(+)=100

2024-10-30 12:14:30====>获取就诊信息:Select Decode(B.急诊,1,'2','1') As visitTypeCode,A.ID As visitNo,to_char(A.开始时间,'yyyymmdd') As visitDate,
                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,'' As wardCode,'' As wardName,'' As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人挂号记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D
                             Where A.Id=B.记录id And A.科室id=C.资源id And A.服务人id=D.资源id
                               And A.id='25A986B5-69B1-1A0C-E064-9CDC71ADEB60'
                            Union All
                            Select '3' As visitTypeCode,A.ID As visitNo,to_char(A.开始时间,'yyyymmdd') As visitDate,
                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,E.编码 As wardCode,E.简称 As wardName,B.床号 As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人入院记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D,部门 E
                             Where A.Id=B.事件id And A.科室id=C.资源id And A.服务人id=D.资源id And B.病房id=E.资源id(+)
                               And A.id='25A986B5-69B1-1A0C-E064-9CDC71ADEB60'
2024-10-30 12:14:30====>获取诊断信息:Select B.主诉 As chiefCompliant,C.问题名称 As diagName,C.问题编码 As diagCode
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人挂号记录 B,个人问题列表 C
                             Where A.Id=B.记录id And A.Id=C.服务记录id(+)
                               And A.id='25A986B5-69B1-1A0C-E064-9CDC71ADEB60'
                               And Rownum<2
                            Union All
                            Select Distinct '' As chiefCompliant,C.问题名称 As diagName,C.问题编码 As diagCode
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人入院记录 B,个人问题列表 C
                             Where A.Id=B.事件id  And A.Id=C.服务记录id(+) And C.记录性质=2 
                               And A.id='25A986B5-69B1-1A0C-E064-9CDC71ADEB60'
                               And Rownum<2
2024-10-30 12:14:30====>获取检验项目编码:Select D.编码 As labItemCode,D.名称 As labItemName
                              From 个人医嘱记录 A,诊疗项目目录 D
                             Where A.诊疗项目id=D.id
                               And A.事件ID='25A986B5-69B1-1A0C-E064-9CDC71ADEB60'
                               And A.机构id='4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                               And A.组序号 in (5)
                               And A.诊疗类别='C'
                               And (D.撤档时间 Is Null Or D.撤档时间>Sysdate)
